                    function reformatForPTR(url) {
                const [protocol, rest] = url.split('//')
                const [wowhead, affix] = rest.replace('www.', '').split('/')

                return [
                    protocol,
                    [wowhead, 'beta', affix].join('/')
                ].join('//')
            }

            abilityPath = reformatForPTR(abilityPath);
            buffPath = reformatForPTR(buffPath);
            itemPath = reformatForPTR(itemPath);
            npcPath = reformatForPTR(npcPath);

            window.whPtrTooltipInterval = window.whPtrTooltipInterval || setInterval(() => {
                Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('a'))
                    .filter(a => a.href.includes('wowhead') && !a.href.includes('beta'))
                    .forEach(a => {
                        a.href = reformatForPTR(a.href);
                    });
            }, 1500);


        function abilityExternalLink(id) {
            if (id < abilityCutoff)
                return '#';
            if (buffCutoff && id >= buffCutoff)
                return buffPath + (id - buffCutoff);
            return abilityPath + id;
        }

        function abilityExternalLinkForEntry(ability) {
            let linkID = ability.secondaryGameID ? ability.secondaryGameID : ability.guid
            return abilityExternalLink(linkID)
        }

        function buffExternalLink(id) {
            if (id < abilityCutoff)
                return '#';
            if (buffCutoff)
                return `${buffPath}${id - buffCutoff}`;
            return `${buffPath}${id}`; // id can be a string for some games with no buff cutoff.
        }

        function buffExternalLinkForEntry(ability) {
            let linkID = ability.secondaryGameID ? ability.secondaryGameID : ability.guid
            return buffExternalLink(linkID)
        }

        function itemExternalLink(id) {
            return itemPath + id;
        }

        function npcExternalLink(id) {
            return npcPath + id;
        }

        function npcExternalLinkForEntry(actor) {
            let linkID = actor.secondaryGameID ? actor.secondaryGameID : actor.guid
            return npcExternalLink(linkID)
        }

    <script>
        function isClickOnMenu(event, classToLookFor, optionalClass) {
            const targetEvent = (event !== undefined && event !== null) ? event.target : null;
            if (targetEvent !== undefined && targetEvent !== null) {
                const parent = targetEvent.closest('.' + classToLookFor);
                const isClickInsideMenu = targetEvent.classList.contains(classToLookFor) ||
                    (parent !== null && parent !== undefined);
                if (!optionalClass) {
                    return isClickInsideMenu;
                } else {
                    const parentOptional = targetEvent.closest('.' + optionalClass);
                    const isClickInsideOptional = targetEvent.classList.contains(optionalClass) ||
                        (parentOptional !== null && parentOptional !== undefined);
                    return isClickInsideMenu || isClickInsideOptional;
                }
            } else {
                return true;
            }
            return false;
        }

        function openMenu(parentElementClassName, fadedPanelId, clickMenuTestFunction) {
            const parentElement = document.getElementsByClassName(parentElementClassName);
            if (parentElement !== undefined && parentElement !== null && parentElement.length > 0) {
                parentElement[0].classList.add("visible");
            }
            document.removeEventListener('click', onReportDocumentClick);
            document.getElementById(fadedPanelId).classList.add('open');
            document.addEventListener('click', function (event) {
                onReportDocumentClick(event, clickMenuTestFunction, parentElementClassName, fadedPanelId);
            });
        }

        function closeMenu(parentElementClassName, fadedPanelId) {
            const parentElement = document.getElementsByClassName(parentElementClassName);
            if (parentElement !== undefined && parentElement !== null && parentElement.length > 0) {
                parentElement[0].classList.remove("visible");
            }
            document.removeEventListener('click', onReportDocumentClick);
            document.getElementById(fadedPanelId).classList.remove('open');
        }

        function onReportDocumentClick(event, clickMenuTestFunction, parentElementClassName, fadedPanelId) {
            if (!clickMenuTestFunction(event)) {
                const guildOuterWrpList = document.getElementsByClassName(parentElementClassName);
                if (guildOuterWrpList !== undefined && guildOuterWrpList !== null && guildOuterWrpList.length > 0) {
                    closeMenu(parentElementClassName, fadedPanelId, this);
                }
            }
        }
    </script>

                <script>
                    function onClickGuildElement(event) {
                        const guildOuterWrpList = document.getElementsByClassName('guild-reports-menu-outerWrp');
                        if (guildOuterWrpList !== undefined && guildOuterWrpList !== null && guildOuterWrpList.length > 0) {
                            if (guildOuterWrpList[0].classList.contains("visible")) {
                                if (isClickOnMenu(event, 'report-info-button')) {
                                    closeMenu('guild-reports-menu-outerWrp', 'report-view-contents');
                                    return false;
                                }
                            } else {
                                openMenu('guild-reports-menu-outerWrp', 'report-view-contents', isClickOnGuildMenu);
                            }
                        }
                    }

                    function isClickOnGuildMenu(event) {
                        return isClickOnMenu(event, 'report-info-title-wrp', 'report-info-button');
                    }
                </script>

                        function onClickSettingsButton(event) {
                            const guildOuterWrpList = document.getElementsByClassName('report-settings-dropdown');
                            if (guildOuterWrpList !== undefined && guildOuterWrpList !== null && guildOuterWrpList.length > 0) {
                                if (guildOuterWrpList[0].classList.contains("visible")) {
                                    if (isClickOnMenu(event, 'report-settings-btn')) {
                                        closeMenu('report-settings-dropdown', 'report-view-contents');
                                        return false;
                                    }
                                } else {
                                    openMenu('report-settings-dropdown', 'report-view-contents', isClickOnSettingsMenu);
                                }
                            }
                        }

                        function isClickOnSettingsMenu(event) {
                            return isClickOnMenu(event, 'report-settings', 'report-settings-btn');
                        }

                        document.getElementById('report-settings-clickZone').addEventListener('click', function (event) {
                            onClickSettingsButton(event)
                        })
                    </script>
